  <title>Purdue Chinese School</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9146975</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9146975</link>
  <enclosure url="https://se-images.campuslabs.com/clink/images/7b2b21dc-7277-4d0d-9e6c-ccd2597b186f18339274-3e39-44ca-a72a-d3cd3c349d44.png?preset=med-w" length="1" type="image/jpeg" />
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Purdue Chinese School</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>The purpose of this event is to teach children of Chinese backgrounds Chinese literacy including reading, writing, and speaking. Every Saturday morning from 9 am to 12pm during the semester, we gather together and start seven classes in the Krannert Building basement. Many Chinese students or scholars arrive at Purdue each year, it's very easy to find qualified and experienced teachers for each grade of the class. A class consists of 50 minutes of lecturing, 10 minutes break and another 50 minutes of lecture, and some group activities at the end. We also hold midterms and finals following Purdue's academic calendar and arrange student parents as volunteers each week to help younger kids and maintain general security.</p></div>
  <div>
    <p>

<item>
  <title>PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023 (Part 1)</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9205006</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9205006</link>
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023 (Part 1)</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">The PTSC reserves the right to modify this schedule as needed throughout the season. Announcements of any modifications will be sent via email, GroupMe, and will be posted on the website. Check purduetrapandskeet.com for event updates BEFORE planning a visit.</span></em></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Trap and Skeet Practice</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Consists of American trap and skeet practice. At least one trap and one skeet field will be open. Last round of shooters will begin 15 minutes before closing. Five stand open with weather permitting.&nbsp; </span><strong>Open Noon - 6pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Big 50</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp;Amateur Trapshooting Association sponsored event that consists of 50 singles, 50 handicap, 25 pair (50 targets) doubles. Non-ATA shooters are welcome. </span><strong>Registration/Practice @ Noon, ATA Program at 1pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Marathons</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Marathons will run in conjunction with normal practice dates. At least one trap will be designated for the marathon targets at all times during the shoot. ATA members will be able to shoot up to 300 registered targets. Targets must be shot in 100 target segments (100, 200, or 300). All ATA members welcome! </span><strong>Registered targets to be shot from 1-6pm, range opens at 12:30p</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Games and Practice</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">In shotgun sports, many different shooting games have been created that shooters of all levels can enjoy. Games played during the shoot and their rules will be determined by the shoot management/range officer. Normal games include: handicap, doubles trap, 10 birds, Piece Protections, Killers, and Annie Oakley. These games are meant STRICTLY FOR FUN. A practice trap will also be available during these shoots. If a sufficient number of shooters do not sign up to participate in games, only practice will be available. Last round of shooters will begin 15 minutes before closing.&nbsp; Five stand open 3-6p with weather permitting. </span><strong>Open 3-9pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p><strong>August</strong></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Saturday the 19th from Noon-3pm: </span><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">Club Sports B-Involved Fair (Recruitment and Info Event for Students and Staff)&nbsp;</span></em></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Friday the 25th at 6pm: </span><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">Club Callout Meeting</span></em></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Sunday the 27th from Noon-6pm: </span><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">PRIVATE RANGE OPENING FOR NEW AND CURRENT PURDUE STUDENTS&nbsp;</span></em></li>
</ul>

  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Health & Safety Initiative - Fall 2023</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>This will be community wide FSCL programming put on my the council leadership with the help of the advisors. During this programming, students will be given workshops and presentations on many topics that are related to what our students are dealing with each day. Topics include but not limited to Safe Alcohol Use, Substance Use, Body Image &amp; Disordered Eating, Event Planning, Mental Health, Sexual Assault Prevention, and others. Working with both Novak Talks and Purdue affiliated staff and resources, student leaders and general student members will be able to think critically about multiple components of health and safety. This is a very important program that is put on to help students realize how important the safety and health of all members physically, mentally, and emotionally is prioritized.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p></div>

  <div class="p-name summary">Health & Safety Initiative - Fall 2023</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>This will be community wide FSCL programming put on my the council leadership with the help of the advisors. During this programming, students will be given workshops and presentations on many topics that are related to what our students are dealing with each day. Topics include but not limited to Safe Alcohol Use, Substance Use, Body Image &amp; Disordered Eating, Event Planning, Mental Health, Sexual Assault Prevention, and others. Working with both Novak Talks and Purdue affiliated staff and resources, student leaders and general student members will be able to think critically about multiple components of health and safety. This is a very important program that is put on to help students realize how important the safety and health of all members physically, mentally, and emotionally is prioritized.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p></div>

  <title>PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023 (Part 1)</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9205007</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9205007</link>
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023 (Part 1)</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">The PTSC reserves the right to modify this schedule as needed throughout the season. Announcements of any modifications will be sent via email, GroupMe, and will be posted on the website. Check purduetrapandskeet.com for event updates BEFORE planning a visit.</span></em></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Trap and Skeet Practice</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Consists of American trap and skeet practice. At least one trap and one skeet field will be open. Last round of shooters will begin 15 minutes before closing. Five stand open with weather permitting.&nbsp; </span><strong>Open Noon - 6pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Big 50</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp;Amateur Trapshooting Association sponsored event that consists of 50 singles, 50 handicap, 25 pair (50 targets) doubles. Non-ATA shooters are welcome. </span><strong>Registration/Practice @ Noon, ATA Program at 1pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Marathons</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Marathons will run in conjunction with normal practice dates. At least one trap will be designated for the marathon targets at all times during the shoot. ATA members will be able to shoot up to 300 registered targets. Targets must be shot in 100 target segments (100, 200, or 300). All ATA members welcome! </span><strong>Registered targets to be shot from 1-6pm, range opens at 12:30p</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Games and Practice</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">In shotgun sports, many different shooting games have been created that shooters of all levels can enjoy. Games played during the shoot and their rules will be determined by the shoot management/range officer. Normal games include: handicap, doubles trap, 10 birds, Piece Protections, Killers, and Annie Oakley. These games are meant STRICTLY FOR FUN. A practice trap will also be available during these shoots. If a sufficient number of shooters do not sign up to participate in games, only practice will be available. Last round of shooters will begin 15 minutes before closing.&nbsp; Five stand open 3-6p with weather permitting. </span><strong>Open 3-9pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p><strong>August</strong></p>
<ul>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Saturday the 19th from Noon-3pm: </span><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">Club Sports B-Involved Fair (Recruitment and Info Event for Students and Staff)&nbsp;</span></em></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Friday the 25th at 6pm: </span><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">Club Callout Meeting</span></em></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Sunday the 27th from Noon-6pm: </span><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">PRIVATE RANGE OPENING FOR NEW AND CURRENT PURDUE STUDENTS&nbsp;</span></em></li>
</ul>

  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9146976</guid>

  <enclosure url="https://se-images.campuslabs.com/clink/images/7b2b21dc-7277-4d0d-9e6c-ccd2597b186f18339274-3e39-44ca-a72a-d3cd3c349d44.png?preset=med-w" length="1" type="image/jpeg" />
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Purdue Chinese School</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>The purpose of this event is to teach children of Chinese backgrounds Chinese literacy including reading, writing, and speaking. Every Saturday morning from 9 am to 12pm during the semester, we gather together and start seven classes in the Krannert Building basement. Many Chinese students or scholars arrive at Purdue each year, it's very easy to find qualified and experienced teachers for each grade of the class. A class consists of 50 minutes of lecturing, 10 minutes break and another 50 minutes of lecture, and some group activities at the end. We also hold midterms and finals following Purdue's academic calendar and arrange student parents as volunteers each week to help younger kids and maintain general security.</p></div>
  <div>

<item>
  <title>Grandmaster Flash -- CVN RSVP</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9295325</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9295325</link>
  <enclosure url="https://se-images.campuslabs.com/clink/images/1a648c25-23fc-4f73-8843-f5b9d72482b05e7bec75-1320-418d-a0ff-f2f6392869d8.png?preset=med-w" length="1" type="image/jpeg" />
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Grandmaster Flash -- CVN RSVP</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>Who knows what hip-hop would sound like without&nbsp;<a href="http://www.grandmasterflash.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Grandmaster Flash</a>? A musical pioneer in every sense of the word, Flash transformed the turntable into an expressive and complex instrument, and introduced the world to record scratching, beat juggling, and breaks. His mastery of these techniques elevated DJ&rsquo;ing to an art form, while his legendary parties in the South Bronx became the cradle of hip-hop culture.</p>
<p>This audiovisual lecture/demonstration is an educational, entertaining, and interactive experience that takes you on a journey with one of the founding fathers of hip-hop. As the architect of the quick mix theory, Grandmaster Flash will show you how as a teenager, he used his knowledge of electronic repair to experiment with different styles and techniques and bridge the gap between musical genres&mdash;incorporating elements of funk, soul, and disco into his mixes. Now, as we celebrate 50 years of hip-hop, a whole new generation will experience a once in a lifetime hip-hop history lesson from one of the creators and legends in the genre.</p>
<p>Our student volunteer ushers receive free seating to the show. Sign up today! You will receive full day-of-show details the day before the show. Volunteers will need to arrive at&nbsp;<strong>Loeb Playhouse at 6:15pm.</strong>&nbsp;Dress code is professional business casual. Stay for the show, or be released after the crowd slows down.</p>
<p><strong>RSVP by September 20th.</strong></p></div>
  <div>
    <p>
      From <time class="dt-start dtstart" datetime="2023-09-23T18:15:00.0000000-04:00" title="2023-09-23T18:15:00.0000000-04:00">Saturday, September 23, 2023 6:15 PM</time>

    </p>

  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9363307</link>

  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Ganesh Chathurthi</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>This event will be a celebration of the Indian festival Ganesh Chathurthi, marking the birth of the Indian god who represents prosperity and wisdom. This festival is usually celebrated by making and displaying clay idols of the God. In our Ganesh Chathurti event, we will provide all the attendees with play doh to make their own miniature idols of the God and celebrate this festival, away from home, with other students that they share a culture with. During this festival, we offer Indian desserts to our friends and family. We wish to create a similar atmosphere so we will be handing out store-bought Indian desserts. We will also have a small presentation on why the festival is celebrated, its importance and significance today.&nbsp;</p></div>
  <div>
    <p>
      From <time class="dt-start dtstart" datetime="2023-09-24T13:30:00.0000000-04:00" title="2023-09-24T13:30:00.0000000-04:00">Sunday, September 24, 2023 1:30 PM</time>

  <div class="p-description description"><p>A parkour workout hosted by the Parkour and Calisthenics Club! Tuesdays and Thursdays consist of both level 1 and level 2 workouts. Sundays have only level 1 workouts.</p>
<p><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Level 2</span>: Lasting one hour (5:00 pm to 6:00 pm), with a focus on advanced skills. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Begins with a quick warmup, followed by 3-5 different movements, and ending in a cooldown.</span></p>
<p><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Level 1:</span>&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 400;">Lasting one hour (6:00 pm to 7:00 pm, and 4:00 pm to 5:00 pm Sunday), with a focus on building foundational skills and a good base for advanced movements. Begins with a quick warmup, followed by 3-5 different movements, and ending in a cooldown.</span></p></div>

  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Purdue AIChE All Member Meetings</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>Purdue AIChE's All Member Meetings (AMM) are monthly meetings for General Members. These meetings can either be professional, social, or philanthropic. On the professional side, we have invited industry speakers, cultural center representatives, and alumni to teach us about a certain topic. On the social side, we have hosted pumpkin carving and game/trivia events. On the philanthropic side, we have made blankets for NICU babies and dog toys for the campus animal shelter. Our organization always caters food for this meeting. This meeting is held usually the last Monday of each month from 6-7pm in the Forney Hall of Chemical Engineering. To learn more about Purdue AIChE and our events, visit&nbsp;https://engineering.purdue.edu/AIChE.&nbsp;</p></div>

<item>
  <title>Donation Day</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9374367</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9374367</link>
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Donation Day</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>During donation days, members of our organization stand outside of Walmart and ask store patrons to donate purchased items with the intent of taking the items to support marginalized communities. More specifically, these items will be taken on our organization's service trip to the Honduras at the end of the year. We will be asking patrons to purchase and donate items such as toiletries and clothing to support the Honduran community. Members of our organization who volunteer for the Donation Day will be speaking directly to patrons and collecting purchased items from them. After the Donation Day is over, members of our organization will transport the items back to Purdue and store them until they are needed for our service trip.&nbsp;</p></div>
  <div>

<item>
  <title>PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023 (Part 1)</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9205008</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9205008</link>
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023 (Part 1)</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">The PTSC reserves the right to modify this schedule as needed throughout the season. Announcements of any modifications will be sent via email, GroupMe, and will be posted on the website. Check purduetrapandskeet.com for event updates BEFORE planning a visit.</span></em></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Trap and Skeet Practice</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Consists of American trap and skeet practice. At least one trap and one skeet field will be open. Last round of shooters will begin 15 minutes before closing. Five stand open with weather permitting.&nbsp; </span><strong>Open Noon - 6pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Big 50</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp;Amateur Trapshooting Association sponsored event that consists of 50 singles, 50 handicap, 25 pair (50 targets) doubles. Non-ATA shooters are welcome. </span><strong>Registration/Practice @ Noon, ATA Program at 1pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Marathons</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Marathons will run in conjunction with normal practice dates. At least one trap will be designated for the marathon targets at all times during the shoot. ATA members will be able to shoot up to 300 registered targets. Targets must be shot in 100 target segments (100, 200, or 300). All ATA members welcome! </span><strong>Registered targets to be shot from 1-6pm, range opens at 12:30p</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Games and Practice</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">In shotgun sports, many different shooting games have been created that shooters of all levels can enjoy. Games played during the shoot and their rules will be determined by the shoot management/range officer. Normal games include: handicap, doubles trap, 10 birds, Piece Protections, Killers, and Annie Oakley. These games are meant STRICTLY FOR FUN. A practice trap will also be available during these shoots. If a sufficient number of shooters do not sign up to participate in games, only practice will be available. Last round of shooters will begin 15 minutes before closing.&nbsp; Five stand open 3-6p with weather permitting. </span><strong>Open 3-9pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p><strong>August</strong></p>

<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Saturday the 19th from Noon-3pm: </span><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">Club Sports B-Involved Fair (Recruitment and Info Event for Students and Staff)&nbsp;</span></em></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Friday the 25th at 6pm: </span><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">Club Callout Meeting</span></em></li>
<li style="font-weight: 400;" aria-level="1"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Sunday the 27th from Noon-6pm: </span><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">PRIVATE RANGE OPENING FOR NEW AND CURRENT PURDUE STUDENTS&nbsp;</span></em></li>

  <div class="p-name summary">Mid-Autumn Festival Celebration</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>Mid-Autumn Festival is considered to be an important cultural tradition among the Asian community. The entire celebration centers around being with family, friends and loved ones as they enjoy their time together. As HKSA, we would like to organize an event under that similar goal. This involves a dinner, bowling at the PMU, and enjoying the view of the full moon under the night sky while enjoying mooncakes and playing with lanterns and glowsticks, all aimed at allowing even more opportunities to spend quality time together and bond as part of the association.&nbsp;</p></div>

  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9146977</guid>

  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Purdue Chinese School</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>The purpose of this event is to teach children of Chinese backgrounds Chinese literacy including reading, writing, and speaking. Every Saturday morning from 9 am to 12pm during the semester, we gather together and start seven classes in the Krannert Building basement. Many Chinese students or scholars arrive at Purdue each year, it's very easy to find qualified and experienced teachers for each grade of the class. A class consists of 50 minutes of lecturing, 10 minutes break and another 50 minutes of lecture, and some group activities at the end. We also hold midterms and finals following Purdue's academic calendar and arrange student parents as volunteers each week to help younger kids and maintain general security.</p></div>

  <div class="p-name summary">Health & Safety Initiative - Fall 2023</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>This will be community wide FSCL programming put on my the council leadership with the help of the advisors. During this programming, students will be given workshops and presentations on many topics that are related to what our students are dealing with each day. Topics include but not limited to Safe Alcohol Use, Substance Use, Body Image &amp; Disordered Eating, Event Planning, Mental Health, Sexual Assault Prevention, and others. Working with both Novak Talks and Purdue affiliated staff and resources, student leaders and general student members will be able to think critically about multiple components of health and safety. This is a very important program that is put on to help students realize how important the safety and health of all members physically, mentally, and emotionally is prioritized.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p></div>

  <div class="p-description description"><p>This will be community wide FSCL programming put on my the council leadership with the help of the advisors. During this programming, students will be given workshops and presentations on many topics that are related to what our students are dealing with each day. Topics include but not limited to Safe Alcohol Use, Substance Use, Body Image &amp; Disordered Eating, Event Planning, Mental Health, Sexual Assault Prevention, and others. Working with both Novak Talks and Purdue affiliated staff and resources, student leaders and general student members will be able to think critically about multiple components of health and safety.   <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Purdue Chinese School</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>The purpose of this event is to teach children of Chinese backgrounds Chinese literacy including reading, writing, and speaking. Every Saturday morning from 9 am to 12pm during the semester, we gather together and start seven classes in the Krannert Building basement. Many Chinese students or scholars arrive at Purdue each year, it's very easy to find qualified and experienced teachers for each grade of the class. A class consists of 50 minutes of lecturing, 10 minutes break and another 50 minutes of lecture, and some group activities at the end. We also hold midterms and finals following Purdue's academic calendar and arrange student parents as volunteers each week to help younger kids and maintain general security.</p></div>

  <title>Briscoe -- CVN RSVP</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9295693</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9295693</link>
  <enclosure url="https://se-images.campuslabs.com/clink/images/486a3361-5a42-4699-b9ff-8d10c241d37386267fa1-d043-499d-a34e-9ce462bae80d.png?preset=med-w" length="1" type="image/jpeg" />
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Briscoe -- CVN RSVP</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>After winning over 6,000 new fans as an opener for <a href="https://noahkahan.com/#/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Noah Kahan</a> last spring at Elliott Hall of Music, pop duo <a href="https://www.briscoetheband.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Briscoe</a> returns to Purdue &ndash; this time as deserving headliners. Led by Truett Heintzelman and Philip Lupton, the band pushes feel-good vibes throughout its eclectic sound, which borrows heavily from the laid-back and lush sounds of 1960s and &rsquo;70s rock, folk, and funk.</p>
<p>Emanating from the live music mecca of Austin, Texas, Briscoe earned its national recognition opening for and sharing stages with the likes of <a href="https://www.deathcabforcutie.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Death Cab for Cutie</a>, <a href="https://www.mymorningjacket.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">My Morning Jacket</a>, and <a href="https://tameimpala.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Tame Impala</a>&mdash;all while earning degrees from The University of Texas. Watch out for Briscoe&rsquo;s debut LP produced by <a href="https://www.bradleytime.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Brad Cook</a> (Bon Iver, The War on Drugs, Nathaniel Rateliff &amp; The Night Sweats).</p>
<p>Our student volunteer ushers receive free seating to the show. Sign up today! You will receive full day-of-show details the day before the show. Volunteers will need to arrive at&nbsp;<strong>Loeb Playhouse at 6:15pm.</strong>&nbsp;Dress code is professional business casual. Stay for the show, or be released after the crowd slows down.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p><strong>RSVP by October 9th.</strong></p>

<item>
  <title>PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023 (Part 1)</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9205009</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9205009</link>
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023 (Part 1)</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">The PTSC reserves the right to modify this schedule as needed throughout the season. Announcements of any modifications will be sent via email, GroupMe, and will be posted on the website. Check purduetrapandskeet.com for event updates BEFORE planning a visit.</span></em></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Trap and Skeet Practice</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Consists of American trap and skeet practice. At least one trap and one skeet field will be open. Last round of shooters will begin 15 minutes before closing. Five stand open with weather permitting.&nbsp; </span><strong>Open Noon - 6pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Big 50</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp;Amateur Trapshooting Association sponsored event that consists of 50 singles, 50 handicap, 25 pair (50 targets) doubles. Non-ATA shooters are welcome. </span><strong>Registration/Practice @ Noon, ATA Program at 1pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Marathons</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Marathons will run in conjunction with normal practice dates. At least one trap will be designated for the marathon targets at all times during the shoot. ATA members will be able to shoot up to 300 registered targets. Targets must be shot in 100 target segments (100, 200, or 300). All ATA members welcome! </span><strong>Registered targets to be shot from 1-6pm, range opens at 12:30p</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Games and Practice</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">In shotgun sports, many different shooting games have been created that shooters of all levels can enjoy. Games played during the shoot and their rules will be determined by the shoot management/range officer. Normal games include: handicap, doubles trap, 10 birds, Piece Protections, Killers, and Annie Oakley. These games are meant STRICTLY FOR FUN. A practice trap will also be available during these shoots. If a sufficient number of shooters do not sign up to participate in games, only practice will be available. Last round of shooters will begin 15 minutes before closing.&nbsp; Five stand open 3-6p with weather permitting. </span><strong>Open 3-9pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>

  <title>Purdue Chinese School</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9146979</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9146979</link>
  <enclosure url="https://se-images.campuslabs.com/clink/images/7b2b21dc-7277-4d0d-9e6c-ccd2597b186f18339274-3e39-44ca-a72a-d3cd3c349d44.png?preset=med-w" length="1" type="image/jpeg" />
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Purdue Chinese School</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>The purpose of this event is to teach children of Chinese backgrounds Chinese literacy including reading, writing, and speaking. Every Saturday morning from 9 am to 12pm during the semester, we gather together and start seven classes in the Krannert Building basement. Many Chinese students or scholars arrive at Purdue each year, it's very easy to find qualified and experienced teachers for each grade of the class. A class consists of 50 minutes of lecturing, 10 minutes break and another 50 minutes of lecture, and some group activities at the end. We also hold midterms and finals following Purdue's academic calendar and arrange student parents as volunteers each week to help younger kids and maintain general security.</p></div>

<item>
  <title>PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023 (Part 1)</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9205010</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9205010</link>
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023 (Part 1)</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>PTSC Range Schedule Fall 2023</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><em><span style="font-weight: 400;">The PTSC reserves the right to modify this schedule as needed throughout the season. Announcements of any modifications will be sent via email, GroupMe, and will be posted on the website. Check purduetrapandskeet.com for event updates BEFORE planning a visit.</span></em></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Trap and Skeet Practice</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Consists of American trap and skeet practice. At least one trap and one skeet field will be open. Last round of shooters will begin 15 minutes before closing. Five stand open with weather permitting.&nbsp; </span><strong>Open Noon - 6pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Big 50</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">&nbsp;Amateur Trapshooting Association sponsored event that consists of 50 singles, 50 handicap, 25 pair (50 targets) doubles. Non-ATA shooters are welcome. </span><strong>Registration/Practice @ Noon, ATA Program at 1pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Marathons</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">ATA Marathons will run in conjunction with normal practice dates. At least one trap will be designated for the marathon targets at all times during the shoot. ATA members will be able to shoot up to 300 registered targets. Targets must be shot in 100 target segments (100, 200, or 300). All ATA members welcome! </span><strong>Registered targets to be shot from 1-6pm, range opens at 12:30p</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">Games and Practice</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-weight: 400;">In shotgun sports, many different shooting games have been created that shooters of all levels can enjoy. Games played during the shoot and their rules will be determined by the shoot management/range officer. Normal games include: handicap, doubles trap, 10 birds, Piece Protections, Killers, and Annie Oakley. These games are meant STRICTLY FOR FUN. A practice trap will also be available during these shoots. If a sufficient number of shooters do not sign up to participate in games, only practice will be available. Last round of shooters will begin 15 minutes before closing.&nbsp; Five stand open 3-6p with weather permitting. </span><strong>Open 3-9pm</strong></p>
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p><strong>August</strong></p>

  <title>Fall 2023 League of Legends Intramurals</title>
  <guid>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9119926</guid>
  <link>https://boilerlink.purdue.edu/event/9119926</link>
  <enclosure url="https://se-images.campuslabs.com/clink/images/63b76611-f4f2-44a5-86c9-53355fdf7f7aaae0058c-b3c9-4fa2-a534-5f0d1fac74f6.png?preset=med-w" length="1" type="image/jpeg" />
  <description><![CDATA[<div class="h-event vevent">
  <div class="p-name summary">Fall 2023 League of Legends Intramurals</div>
  <div class="p-description description"><p>Presenting Purdue League of Legends Club 8-Week Intramurals&mdash;an exciting event where teams can showcase their skills and compete for the top spot in two engaging phases: Seasonal Play and the Single Elimination Playoff Tournament. We've carefully crafted every aspect of this tournament to ensure an enriching experience for all participants.</p>
<p>During the Seasonal Play phase, teams will have the opportunity to engage in a series of matches, each lasting one game. These matches are scheduled for Wednesday nights at 9pm EST, although we are flexible and willing to accommodate teams by adjusting the timing as needed.</p>
<p>Following the Seasonal Play phase, teams will enter the Single Elimination Playoff Tournament, where their seedings will be determined by their performance in the previous phase. This tournament will feature best-of-three matches, allowing teams to strategize and showcase their prowess. The exact game times for these matches will be mutually agreed upon by the participating teams, ensuring convenience and fairness.</p>
<p>To participate in intramurals, there is a registration fee of $5 per person. However, we offer a special incentive for pre-made teams consisting of 5-6 players&mdash;a $10 discount on their total registration fees. This encourages friends to come together and form cohesive teams, all while enjoying the added benefit of reduced costs.</p>
<p>We understand the significance of recognizing teams for their efforts and achievements. Therefore, we have arranged prizing for the top three teams.</p>
<p>This 8-Week Intramural League provides a platform for participants to showcase their talents, create lasting memories, and immerse themselves in the spirit of friendly competition. We invite you to register now and join us in celebrating the joy of gaming at its finest.</p></div>
